====================================================================================================
CDA6 UDS COMMAND REFERENCE - FOR USE WITH ALFAOBD
Generated from 52 decrypted CDA6 module databases
====================================================================================================

USAGE IN ALFAOBD:
  1. Connect to vehicle via J2534/ELM327
  2. Select the target module
  3. Open UDS Terminal
  4. Send the hex commands listed below

COMMAND FORMAT:
  22 XX XX        = Read Data By Identifier (DID)
  2E XX XX [data] = Write Data By Identifier
  31 01 XX XX     = Start Routine
  31 02 XX XX     = Get Routine Results
  31 03 XX XX     = Stop Routine
  2F XX XX XX     = Input/Output Control By Identifier
  27 XX           = Security Access (request seed)
  10 01/02/03     = Session Control (default/programming/extended)
